<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lulkoek.html>lulkoek</a> (9418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lullen.html>lullen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk nonsense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koek.html>koek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lulkoek.html>lulkoek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bullshit.html>bullshit</a>, poppycock, nonsense</li></ol>

***lullen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lullen.html>lullen</a> (6299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leh₂-</i> (expressive root), presumably an onomatopoeia. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lāmentum</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λῆρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lêros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάλος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lálos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάσκω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láskō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lullen.html>lullen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To talk/tell nonsense</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To mumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be occupied uttering one of the above noises</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To loiter, waste time, hang around unproductively</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be weak / useless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lullo.html>lullo</a> (74582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1980s or early 1990s. Popularised in 1996 by Jiskefet. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lul.html>lul</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a>, cock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-o</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">typical denominative suffix in several <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slangs</a>, particularly Turbotaal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lullo.html>lullo</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lullo.html>lullo</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lullo.html>lullootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a></span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">dickhead</span>, an <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">generic insult, usually for males</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lunchbox.html>lunchbox</a> (91004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">box</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunchbox.html>lunchbox</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lunchboxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A container for transporting meals, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person or object constantly at one's side (in the manner of a <a href = vnd.unilang:lunchbox.html>lunchbox</a>).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The male genitals when enclosed in clothing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Asia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a> packaged in a disposable box to be <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> away to eat.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A luggable; an early laptop computer, usually a unit with a handle and a fold-out keyboard.
<ul><li><b>1988</b>, <i>PC <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>Mag</a></i> (volume 7, number 17, 11 October 1988, page 93)
<dl><dd>You'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> find a mix among clamshell <a href = vnd.unilang:laptops.html>laptops</a> for strong laps, <b>lunchboxes</b>, and sewing-machine configurations; the latter two <a href = vnd.unilang:designs.html>designs</a> typically have detachable <a href = vnd.unilang:keyboards.html>keyboards</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2004</b>, Scott Mueller, <i>Upgrading and Repairing <a href = vnd.unilang:laptops.html>Laptops</a></i> (page 20)
<dl><dd>The performance difference between desktops and <b>lunchboxes</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> practically nil.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A simple portable transmitter sometimes used in phreaking.</li>
<li>A cocktail made with <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>, orange juice, and almond liqueur.</li></ol>

***lunchen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lunchen.html>lunchen</a> (2364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a></i>, presumably short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">luncheon</i>, which see.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunchen.html>lunchen</a></strong>
</p>

***lunt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a> (90997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lont.html>lont</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lunts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A slow-burning match or torch.
<ul><li><b>1844</b>, E. A. Friedlænder (translator), <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>Amber</a> Witch</i> [1838, Abraham Schweidler (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wilhelm_Meinhold" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wilhelm Meinhold">Wilhelm Meinhold</a>), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Schweidler, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> Bernsteinhexe</i>], <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=nTpkAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA90amp;dq=%22a+lunt%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22a%20lunt%22amp;f=false">page 90</a>,
<dl><dd>In the mean time, however, he himself (understand; the young <i>Nobilis</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> seen that a fine smoke issued from the nostrils of the <a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a>, and as he stooped down, he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> immediately pulled forth a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></b>, almost of a finger's length, the which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> yet burning, and which a knave <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> privily poked into his nostrils with a needle.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1969</b>,  Robert <a href = vnd.unilang:nye.html>Nye</a>,  <cite>Tales I <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>Told</a> My Mother</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>Bent</a> down and saw I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> right. A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></b> up the bugger’s nose. A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Doctor Copper. Almost as long as your left forefinger, yes, <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> his visitor. Still burning.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1999</b>, Igorʹ Mikhaĭlovich Dʹi͡akonov, <i>The Paths of History</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=tft0FCEzFJcCamp;pg=PA149amp;dq=%22a+lunt%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22a%20lunt%22amp;f=false">page 149</a>,
<dl><dd>The gunpowder <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stamped into the tube, then a lead ball <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> put into the muzzle, a wad <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stamped <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> it, and the charge <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> set fire to by a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></b> through the lower hole.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Smoke with flames, especially from a pipe.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lunt.html>lunt</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lunts</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lunting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lunted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To emit smoke.
<ul><li><b>18th c</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Burns" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Burns">Robert Burns</a>, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:twa.html>Twa</a> Dogs</i>, <b>1822</b>, <i>The Poetical Works of Robert Burns</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=RjVYAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PA28amp;dq=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;f=false">page 28</a>,
<dl><dd>The <b>lunting</b> pipe, and sneeshing mill, / Are handed round wi' right gude-will;</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1832</b>, <i>Tait's Edinburgh Magazine</i>, Volume 2, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=fOkRAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA377amp;dq=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;f=false">page 377</a>,
<dl><dd>My conscience! ye lent a ready hand in the brulzie; but what can <a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a>'e set the <a href = vnd.unilang:magazines.html>Magazines</a> a-<b>lunting</b>? it's a mystery <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>' <a href = vnd.unilang:mysteries.html>mysteries</a>.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Especially as it's their game to set everybody a-<b>lunting</b>, and keep out of the conflagration themselves.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To walk while smoking a pipe.
<ul><li><b>2014</b>, Robert P. Wills, <i>Tales From A Second Hand <a href = vnd.unilang:wand.html>Wand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:shoppen.html>Shoppe</a></i>, Book 1: They <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>Best</a> of Gnomes, They <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:worst.html>Worst</a> of Gnomes, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com.au/books?id=t2GuBgAAQBAJamp;pg=PA278amp;dq=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22lunted%22%7C%22lunting%22amp;f=false">page 278</a>,
<dl><dd>“<b>Lunting</b>?” interrupted <a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a>, eyebrow raised.</dd>
<dd>Grimbledung shrugged, “It's a good and proper word”, he raised an eyebrow back, "it just doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> get used that much."</dd>
<dd><a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a> smirked, “Go on then, with your <b>lunting</b>.”</dd>
<dd>He let out a sigh. "As I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> saying, <i>I</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sitting there when a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:minotaur.html>Minotaur</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> <b>lunting</b> up." He paused for a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>, "Pipe in mouth, walking along", he winked at <a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***lurch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a> (56798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally a nautical term, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:lacher.html>lacher</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to let go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lurches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A sudden or unsteady movement.
<dl><dd><i>the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></b> of a ship, or of a drunkard</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1898</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J._Meade_Falkner" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J. Meade Falkner">J. Meade Falkner</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moonfleet" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Moonfleet">Moonfleet</a> Chapter 4
<dl><dd>Yet I hoped by grouting at the earth below it to be able to dislodge the stone at the side; but while I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> considering how <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> to begin, the candle flickered, the <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> a sudden <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></b> to one side, and I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> left in darkness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lurches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make such a sudden, unsteady movement.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">lurcāre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lurches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To swallow or eat greedily; to devour; hence, to swallow up.
<ul><li><b>1625</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Bacon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Francis Bacon">Francis Bacon</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Essays_of_Francis_Bacon/XLV_Of_Building" class="extiw" title="s:The Essays of Francis Bacon/XLV Of Building">Of Building</a></i>
<dl><dd>Too far off from great cities, which may hinder business; too near them, which <b>lurcheth</b> all provisions, and maketh everything dear.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">lourche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deceived, embarrassed; also the name of a game</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The French term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seemingly from dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lurz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left-handed, deceptive, wrong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lurtaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">left; left-handed; crooked; <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a>; warped; underhanded; deceitful; limping</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lirt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lurches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An old game played with dice and <a href = vnd.unilang:counters.html>counters</a>; a variety of the game of tables.</li>
<li>A double score in <a href = vnd.unilang:cribbage.html>cribbage</a> for the winner when his/her adversary <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> left in the <a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a>.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Walpole and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Lady Blandford <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> cried her <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> out on losing a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">lurches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">lurched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To leave someone in the <a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a>; to cheat.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by South and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Never deceive or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lurch.html>lurch</a></b> the sincere communicant.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rob.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1608–1609</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coriolanus" class="extiw" title="w:Coriolanus">The Tragedy of Coriolanus</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. ***lusk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a> (103424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lǫskr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak, idle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laskwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sluggish, dull, lazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lēyd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to let, subside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lasch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flabby, loose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">lasch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:las.html>las</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tired, dull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lush</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lazy or slothful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> full; ripe</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lusk.html>lusk</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lusks</b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lustuz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">little</i>, regional German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lütt</i> and German (archaic) <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lützel</i>.

***luxe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:luxe.html>luxe</a> (4692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:luxe.html>luxe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">luxus</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The first part of typical compounds with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luxe.html>luxe</a></i> (e.g. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">luxe-editie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">luxury edition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">luxevilla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">luxury-mansion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ...) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> reinterpreted as an adjective, instead of a noun.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luxe.html>luxe</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:luxer.html>luxer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luxe.html>luxe</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">luxest</b>)
</p>

***lychee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a> (103412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">荔枝</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lai<sup>6</sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:zi.html>zi</a><sup>1</sup></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">litchi</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lychees.html>lychees</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Chinese tropical fruit tree <i>Litchi chinensis</i>, of the soapberry family.</li>
<li>That tree's bright red oval fruit with a single stone surrounded by a fleshy white aril.</li>
<li>A soft pink-red colour, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a> rind (also called <a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a> red).
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a> colour: <span style="background-color:DC5349; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lychee.html>lychee</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a> (2569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">māget</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*magath</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*magaþs</i>. <div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Dutch Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:maagdenvlies" class="extiw" title="w:nl:maagdenvlies"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagdenvlies.html>maagdenvlies</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:maagdenvlies" class="extiw" title="w:nl:maagdenvlies">Wikipedia <sup>nl</sup></a></span></div>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagd.html>maagd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">virgin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vlies.html>vlies</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fleece, membrane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagdenvlies.html>maagdenvlies</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagdenvlies.html>maagdenvliezen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maagdenvliesje.html>maagdenvliesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The hymen, a membrane which occludes the <a href = vnd.unilang:vagina.html>vagina</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in traditional thinking supposed to remain intact only in virgin females.</li></ol>

***maal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a> (3133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*māl</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mēlą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*meh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to measure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mahl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meal</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">mål</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mael</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mēlą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mark, sign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*melh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark color</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with compare Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mæl</i>, Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">mál</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ornament (on a sword)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Gothic <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌴𐌻</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mēl</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">writing, scripture</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Welsh <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">melyn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yellow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mė́las</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέλας</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mélas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dark-colored, black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maaltje.html>maaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mael</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">male</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">māla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mēlō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young cow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)melh₁-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">míl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μῆλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mêlon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lamb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> , <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Breton language"><a href = vnd.unilang:breton.html>Breton</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="br">mil</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">animal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Armenian language">Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="hy">մալ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheep; mutton; wether; cattle; livestock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sorani" class="extiw" title="w:Sorani">Central Kurdish</a></span> <i class="ku-Arab mention" lang="ckb">ماڵ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ckb-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mall</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">livestock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***maalstroom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maalstroom.html>maalstroom</a> (35891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stroom.html>stroom</a></i>. First attested in the 16th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maalstroom.html>maalstroom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maalstroom.html>maalstromen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maalstroom.html>maalstroompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An aquatic vortex, <a href = vnd.unilang:maelstrom.html>maelstrom</a>, large whirlpool; especially a tidal vortex.
<ul><li><b>1769</b>, Charles <a href = vnd.unilang:papillon.html>Papillon</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:algemeen.html>Algemeen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> beredenerent <a href = vnd.unilang:woordenboek.html>woordenboek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> natuurlyke <a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>historie</a></i>, tr. by Valmont <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Bomare from French, publ. by Abraham Blussé amp; son, page 846.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> grootſte <b>maalſtroom</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kent.html>kent</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Noorweegſche <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>Zee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzekert.html>verzekert</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> hy <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twintig.html>twintig</a> uuren in <a href = vnd.unilang:omtrek.html>omtrek</a> beſlaat; hy <a href = vnd.unilang:zwelgt.html>zwelgt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zes.html>zes</a> uuren <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> hy in zynen <a href = vnd.unilang:omtrek.html>omtrek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontmoet.html>ontmoet</a>, Water, Walviſſchen <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schepen.html>Schepen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> hy <a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervolgens.html>vervolgens</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:gedurende.html>gedurende</a> dezelve uitgeſtrektheid <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> tyd <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weder.html>weder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> hy ingezwolgen <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The largest <b><a href = vnd.unilang:maelstrom.html>maelstrom</a></b>, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the one of the Norwegian Sea, one insists that it <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> more than twenty <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> in circumference; it swallows during six <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> everything in that it <a href = vnd.unilang:encounters.html>encounters</a> in its circumference, water, whales and schips, and it subsequently reemits everything again during that same expanse of time, what it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> swallowed in.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of vortex.
<ul><li>Novalis (Georg Philipp Friedrich Freiherr von Hardenberg), "<a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweest.html>geweest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>", tr. by Jan <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>Wit</a> from German, <a href = vnd.unilang:couplet.html>couplet</a> 2.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mâent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mānoth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mēnōþs</i>, from a derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mḗh₁n̥s</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moon, month</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***maandelijks.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maandelijks.html>maandelijks</a> (31740)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maendelijx</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maand.html>maand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">month</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijks</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maandelijks.html>maandelijks</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>monthly, related to a month, occurring during a month or every month</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">māre</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mar</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mer.html>mer</a></i>, apheretic variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nemaer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nemāre</i>, from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">newaer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">neware</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">except, however, only</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ne <a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***maarschalk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maarschalk.html>maarschalk</a> (21875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maerschalc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maerscalc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">marscalc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse, mare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schalk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marechaussee.html>marechaussee</a></i>.
<span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maarschalk.html>maarschalk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maarschalken.html>maarschalken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maarschalk.html>maarschalkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***maat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maat.html>maat</a> (1054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></i>, which still exists in parallel with this form. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*māta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mētō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li>rhythm, beat</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a borrowing of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">māt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">māte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">*gimato</i>, of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:West Germanic languages">West Germanic</a></span> origin, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gamatjô</i>, itself from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ga-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matjô</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*matiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">gimazzo</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mate.html>mate</a></i>.

***macadamia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a> (81650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>Macadamia</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">macadamias</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An evergreen tree, of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>Macadamia</a></i>, native to Australia and cultivated in Hawaii.</li>
<li>The fruit of this tree; the <a href = vnd.unilang:macadamia.html>macadamia</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

***macaw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:macaw.html>macaw</a> (68898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:macao.html>macao</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Tupian languages">Tupian</a></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:macaw.html>macaw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">macaws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various <a href = vnd.unilang:parrots.html>parrots</a> of the genera <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ara.html>Ara</a></i>, <i>Anodorhynchus</i>, <i>Cyanopsitta</i>, <i>Orthopsittaca</i>, <i>Primolius</i> and <i>Diopsittaca</i> of Central and South America, including the largest <a href = vnd.unilang:parrots.html>parrots</a> and characterized by long sabre-shaped <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>, curved powerful <a href = vnd.unilang:bills.html>bills</a>, and usually brilliant plumage.</li></ol>
</body>
